<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tun, cask; <a href = vnd.unilang:whale.html>whale</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:see.html>see</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:there.html>there</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:although.html>Although</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:origin.html>origin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:obscure.html>obscure</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> sometimes-cited <a href = vnd.unilang:association.html>association</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">orcus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">underworld</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> folk-etymology.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">orcas</b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:orca.html>orca</a></strong></b>)

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Translingualism" class="extiw" title="w:Translingualism">translingual</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mul">Orchideae</i>, coined <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linnaeus" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Linnaeus">Linnaeus</a> based <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">orchis</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄρχις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">órkhis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>

***orgel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orgel.html>orgel</a> (21842)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">orgele</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">orgene</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">organa</i>, plural <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">organum</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὄργανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">órganon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanish.html>Spanish</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">huracán</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" class="extiw" title="w:Taíno language">Taíno</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tnq">juracán</i>; cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">ouragan</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hurricane.html>hurricane</a></i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:originally.html>originally</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hurricano</i>); <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Orkan</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a>.

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> *<i>-tra</i> denoting "<a href = ***orthodontist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orthodontist.html>orthodontist</a> (36815)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:orthodontist.html>orthodontist</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:orthodontie.html>orthodontie</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ist</i>. 
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
